            <section class="media-item">
             <div class="media-item__summary size--large">
              <header class="summary-header">
               <p class="category">
                <a class="js-tealium-tracking" data-tracking="mpos=center&amp;mid=b_top_hero&amp;lindex=1&amp;lcol=item_solo" href="https://www.politico.com/states/new-york" target="_blank">
                 New York
                </a>
               </p>
              </header>
              <h3 class="headline">
               <a class="js-tealium-tracking" data-tracking="mpos=center&amp;mid=b_top_hero&amp;lindex=1&amp;lcol=item_solo" href="https://www.politico.com/news/2021/03/07/cuomo-crisis-management-playbook-474191" target="_top">
                Cuomo leans on crisis management playbook as walls close in
               </a>
              </h3>
              <p class="dek">
               The New York Democrat’s reign as "America’s governor" may have come to an end, but it’s far less certain that his actual governorship is end-stage.
              </p>
              <div class="meta">
               <div class="meta__details">
                <p class="authors">
                 By
                 <span class="vcard">
                  <a class="url fn js-tealium-tracking" data-tracking="mpos=center&amp;mid=b_top_hero&amp;lindex=1&amp;lcol=item_solo" href="https://www.politico.com/staff/david-siders" rel="author" target="_top">
                   David Siders
                  </a>
                 </span>
                 and
                 <span class="vcard">
                  <a class="url fn js-tealium-tracking" data-tracking="mpos=center&amp;mid=b_top_hero&amp;lindex=1&amp;lcol=item_solo" href="https://www.politico.com/staff/anna-gronewold" rel="author" target="_top">
                   Anna Gronewold
                  </a>
                 </span>
                </p>
               </div>
              </div>
             </div>

            <div class="media-item__image">
             <div class="media-item__image-wrapper">
              <a class="js-tealium-tracking" data-tracking="mpos=center&amp;mid=z_news_well&amp;lindex=1&amp;lcol=item_solo" href="https://www.politico.com/news/2021/03/05/biden-war-powers-congress-473843" target="_top">
               <picture data-lazy-img="true">
                <source data-lazy="https://static.politico.com/dims4/default/8b08f75/2147483647/resize/817x/quality/90/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fstatic.politico.com%2F63%2F3b%2F26c7aad6400da931bf3097783b04%2Fap21063809989065.png" media="(min-width: 1279px)">

                  <source data-lazy="https://static.politico.com/dims4/default/22b2681/2147483647/resize/979x/quality/90/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fstatic.politico.com%2F63%2F3b%2F26c7aad6400da931bf3097783b04%2Fap21063809989065.png" media="(min-width: 767px)">

                     <img alt="President Joe Biden during a virtual call in the Roosevelt Room at the White House, Thursday, March 4, 2021." data-lazy-img="https://static.politico.com/63/3b/26c7aad6400da931bf3097783b04/ap21063809989065.png" title="President Joe Biden during a virtual call in the Roosevelt Room at the White House, Thursday, March 4, 2021."/>

            <div class="media-item__summary">
             <h3 class="headline">
              <a class="js-tealium-tracking" data-tracking="mpos=center&amp;mid=z_news_well&amp;lindex=1&amp;lcol=item_solo" href="https://www.politico.com/news/2021/03/05/biden-war-powers-congress-473843" target="_top">
               Biden backs new war powers vote in Congress, White House says
              </a>
             </h3>
             <p class="dek">
              Facing a bipartisan push to sunset decades-old authorizations, the president will pursue "a narrow and specific framework" to rein in open-ended conflicts.
             </p>
             <div class="meta">
